<h3><a id="user-content-stack-unwinding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#stack-unwinding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Stack Unwinding</h3>
<ul>
<li>Every object has an owner, the stack</li>
<li>Like when returning from functions (go up the stack)</li>
<li>Stack unwinding is the process of exiting the calling frames in the search for an exception handler</li>
<li>If a new exception is thrown during stack unwinding and not caught in the function that threw it, <code>terminate()</code> is called</li>
<li>In destructor, resources might not be released properly if there is exception</li>
<li>All STL guarantee that their destructors are non-throwing</li>
<li>RAII: Resource Acquisition is Initialisation
<ul>
<li>Encapsulates resources inside objects</li>
<li>Acquire resources using constructors</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Use smart pointers because they are owning</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-exception-safety" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#exception-safety"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Exception Safety</h3>
<ul>
<li>An exception specification is part of a function's interface
<ul>
<li><code>void push() noexcept;</code> - Will not throw exception</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Allows throwing exception but must be handled inside the function</li>
<li>Levels of exception safety
<ul>
<li><strong>No-throw guarantee</strong>: also known as failure transparency, operations are guaranteed to succeed and satisfy all requirements even in the presence of exceptional situations. If an exception occurs, it will be handled internally and not observed by clients</li>
<li><strong>Strong exception safety</strong>: also known as commit or rollback semantics, operations can fail, but failed operations are guaranteed to have no side effects so all data retain original values</li>
<li><strong>Basic exception safety</strong>: also known as no-leak guarantee, partial execution of failed operations can cause side effects, but all invariants are preserved and no resources are leaked. Any stored data will contain valid values, even if data has different values now from before the exception</li>
<li><strong>No exception safety</strong>: No guarantees are made</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-lifetimes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#lifetimes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Lifetimes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Lifetime: the period of time in which memory is allocated for an object</li>
<li>Different kinds of objects:
<ul>
<li>Static objects: allocated in a global (static) area</li>
<li>Local (or automatic or stack) objects</li>
<li>Heap objects</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Named objects: (named by the programmer): their lifetimes determined by their scope</li>
<li>Heap objects (unnamed objects): their lifetimes determined by the programmer</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-local-objects" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#local-objects"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Local Objects</h4>
<ul>
<li>Primitive objects are not initialised by default</li>
<li>Class objects are initialised by constructors</li>
<li>Memory management done by the compiler</li>
<li>Every object inaccessible at its closing <code>}</code></li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-temporary-objects" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#temporary-objects"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Temporary Objects</h4>
<ul>
<li>Unnamed objects created on the stack by the compiler</li>
<li>Used during reference initialization and during evaluation of the throw expression</li>
<li>There are two exceptions in the destruction of full-expressions
<ul>
<li>The expression appears as an initializer for a declaration defining an object: the temporary object is destroyed when the initialization is complete</li>
<li>A reference is bound to a temporary object: the temporary object is destroyed at the end of the reference's lifetime</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-static-objects" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#static-objects"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Static Objects</h4>
<ul>
<li>4 categories of objects:
<ul>
<li>Local static objects</li>
<li>Global objects</li>
<li>Namespace objects</li>
<li>Class static objects</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Lifetime: created when functioin is called
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>std::stack&lt;<span class="pl-k">int</span>&gt; s; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> global</span>
<span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">X</span> {
  std::queue&lt;<span class="pl-k">short</span>&gt; q; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> namespace</span>
}
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Y</span> {
  <span class="pl-k">static</span> std::list&lt;<span class="pl-k">char</span>&gt; l; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> class static</span>
};</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-heap-or-free-store-objects" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#heap-or-free-store-objects"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Heap (or Free-Store) Objects</h4>
<ul>
<li>Allocated via <code>new</code> and persist until deleted via <code>delete</code></li>
<li>For array use <code>delete []</code></li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-smart-pointers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#smart-pointers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Smart Pointers</h3>
<ul>
<li>Motivations: efficient, avoid memory leak, avoid double free and dangling pointers</li>
<li>Using reference counting</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-c11-smart-pointers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#c11-smart-pointers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>C++11 Smart Pointers</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-unique_ptr" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#unique_ptr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><code>unique_ptr</code></h4>
<ul>
<li><code>unique_ptr</code> owns the object to which it points to</li>
<li>The underlying object always owned by one owner only</li>
<li>Copy constructor and assignment disabled</li>
<li>Move used to transfer ownership</li>
<li>2 unique_ptr should not hold ownership to the same heap object</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-shared_ptr" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#shared_ptr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><code>shared_ptr</code></h4>
<ul>
<li>Allows multiple pointers to point to the same object</li>
<li>The pointer-to object destroyed when the last pointer goes out of scoope</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-weak_ptr" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#weak_ptr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><code>weak_ptr</code></h4>
<ul>
<li>Points to an object managed by a shared_ptr without incrementing the reference-count</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-week-6" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#week-6"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Week 6</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-constants" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#constants"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Constants</h3>
<ul>
<li>2 notions of immutability
<ul>
<li><code>const</code>: A promise not to change this value</li>
<li><code>constexpr</code>: An indication for it to be evaluated at compile time
<ul>
<li>expression might be <code>constexpr</code> even if not specified</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Aggreagate classes: all its members are public, no constructors, no in-class initializer</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">Data</span> {
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> ival;
  string s;
};</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-templates-overview" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#templates-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Templates Overview</h3>
<ul>
<li>Static polymorphism: compile-time
<ul>
<li>Function overloading</li>
<li>Templates: polymorphical across unrelated types</li>
<li>STL containers, iterators and algorithms are templates</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Dynamic polymorphism: runtime
<ul>
<li>Virtual functions are polymorphic across types related by inheritance</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Generic Programming</strong>
<ul>
<li>Generalising software components so that they are independent of any particular type</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Funtion Templates</strong>
<ul>
<li>A function template is a prescription for the compiler to generate particular instances of a function varying by type
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
T <span class="pl-en">min</span>(T a, T b) {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> a &lt; b ? a : b;
}</pre></div>
</li>
<li>Template can take in 2 type of parameters: type and non-type</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-template-parameters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#template-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Template Parameters</h3>
<ul>
<li>Inside the function is just depends on T</li>
<li>T is the <strong>template type parameter</strong></li>
<li>Placeholder for any built-in or user-defined type</li>
<li>Differenet instances of the function generated depends on when the function is called</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-instantiation" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#instantiation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Instantiation</h3>
<ul>
<li>Inclusion Compilation Model
<ul>
<li>Templates in header files and compile only .cpp files</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-template-argument-deduction" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#template-argument-deduction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Template Argument Deduction</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-name-resolution" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#name-resolution"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Name Resolution</h4>
<ul>
<li>2 parties involved about a function template: designer and client</li>
<li>2-step lookup in name resolution:
<ul>
<li>Type-independent names: resolved at the definition of template - designer provides the declarations</li>
<li>Type-dependent names: resolved at the point of instantiation - client provides the declarations</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>3 kinds of conversions:
<ul>
<li>lvalue transformation
<ul>
<li>Def: <code>template &lt;typename T&gt; f(T* array) { }</code></li>
<li>Use: <code> int a[] = 1, 2; f(a); // array to pointer</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Qualification conversion (const and volatile)
<ul>
<li>Def: <code>template &lt;typename T&gt; f(const T* array) { }</code></li>
<li>Use: <code>int a[] = 1, 2;</code></li>
<li><code>int *pa = &amp;a; f(pa); // int* =&gt; const int*</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Conversion to a base class from a derived class</li>
<li>Def: <code>template &lt;typename T&gt; void f(Base&lt;T&gt; &amp;a) { }</code></li>
<li>Use
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Derived</span> : <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-en">Base</span>&lt;T&gt; { ... }<span class="pl-ii"></span>
Derived&lt;<span class="pl-k">int</span>&gt; d;
<span class="pl-en">f</span>(d);</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-decltype" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#decltype"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><code>decltype</code></h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-explicit-template-arguments" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#explicit-template-arguments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Explicit Template Arguments</h4>
<ul>
<li>All deducted types for the same template parameter must be the same</li>
<li>Explicit template arguments: override the template argument deduction mechanism by explicitly specifying the types of the arguments to be used</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T, <span class="pl-k">typename</span> U&gt;
<span class="pl-k">auto</span> <span class="pl-en">sum</span>(T a, U b) -&gt; decltype(T{} + U{}) {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> a+b;
}</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>More on <code>decltype</code>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> i;
<span class="pl-en">decltype</span>(i) x; <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> int x: i is a variable</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-specialisation" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#specialisation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Specialisation</h3>
<ul>
<li>Needed for correctness or efficiency</li>
<li>min doesnt work for char* so we can do this</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">typedef</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">char</span>* PCC;
<span class="pl-k">template</span>&lt;&gt; PCC min&lt;PCC&gt;(PCC a, PCC b) {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> (<span class="pl-c1">strcmp</span>(a, b) &lt; <span class="pl-c1">0</span>) ? a : b;
}</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-template-default-arguments" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#template-default-arguments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Template Default Arguments</h4>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T, <span class="pl-k">typename</span> Pred=std::less&lt;T&gt;&gt;
T <span class="pl-en">minTD</span>(T a, T b, Pred cmp = Pred()) {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">cmp</span>(a, b) ? a : b;
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-variadic-templates" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#variadic-templates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Variadic Templates</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>typeinfo<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-k">const</span> T&amp; msg) {
  std::cout &lt;&lt; msg &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
}

<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> A, <span class="pl-k">typename</span>... B&gt;
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">print</span>(A head, B... tail) {
  <span class="pl-c1">print</span>(head);
  <span class="pl-c1">print</span>(tail...);
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-class-templates" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#class-templates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Class Templates</h3>
<ul>
<li>Class names cannot be overloaded in C++</li>
<li>Class template does not have deduction for the functions</li>
<li>The member functions have concrete type</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Stack</span> {
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
  <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">push</span>(<span class="pl-k">const</span> T&amp;);
  <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">pop</span>();
  T&amp; <span class="pl-en">top</span>();
<span class="pl-k">private:</span>
  std::vector&lt;T&gt; stack_;
};</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-instantiation-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#instantiation-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Instantiation</h3>
<ul>
<li>Class template only instantiated once for each type</li>
<li>So the same type shares static variables</li>
<li><strong>Instantiation</strong>: Generation of a class from a template</li>
<li><strong>On-deman Instantiation</strong>: a template is instantiated when an object is defined with a type that is a class tempklate</li>
<li><strong>Lazy instantiation</strong>: only member functions used are instantiated</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-name-resolution-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#name-resolution-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Name Resolution</h4>
<ul>
<li>Same two steps as for function templates</li>
<li>Type-independent names are resolved when the template is defined</li>
<li>Type-dependent names are resolved when the template is instantiated</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-default-arguments" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#default-arguments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Default Arguments</h3>
<ul>
<li>Add <code>typename cont=std::deque&lt;t&gt;</code> in the template</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-friends-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#friends-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Friends</h3>
<ul>
<li>3 kinds of friend declarations:</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-ordinary-friend-functionsclasses" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ordinary-friend-functionsclasses"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Ordinary friend functions/classes</h4>
<ul>
<li>A normal class is a friend of template class</li>
<li>Declare the <code>friend</code> inside template class</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-friend-templates" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#friend-templates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Friend templates</h4>
<ul>
<li>All instantiations of the template are friends</li>
<li><code>template &lt;typename U&gt; friend class Task;</code></li>
<li>one-to-many</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-friend-template-instantiations" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#friend-template-instantiations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Friend template instantiations</h4>
<ul>
<li>one-to-one</li>
<li><code>friend class foobar&lt;T&gt;;</code></li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-week-7" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#week-7"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Week 7</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-member-templates" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#member-templates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Member Templates</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
  std::vector&lt;<span class="pl-k">int</span>&gt; <span class="pl-c1">ivec</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>)
  std::vector&lt;<span class="pl-k">int</span>&gt; ivec0 = ivec;
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> error: different containers</span>
  std::list&lt;<span class="pl-k">int</span>&gt; ilist0 = ivec;
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> ok: ctor exists</span>
  std::list&lt;<span class="pl-k">int</span>&gt; <span class="pl-c1">ilist</span>(ivec.<span class="pl-c1">begin</span>(), ivec.<span class="pl-c1">end</span>());
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> ok: member exists</span>
  ilist.<span class="pl-c1">assign</span>(ivec.<span class="pl-c1">begin</span>(), ivec.<span class="pl-c1">end</span>()); ok?
}</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>If different type for the container, the constructors do not work, so need to declare with template too</li>
<li>Template function inside template class
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T2, <span class="pl-k">typename</span> CONT2&gt;
<span class="pl-en">Stack</span>(<span class="pl-k">const</span> Stack&lt;T2, CONT2&gt;&amp;);</pre></div>
</li>
<li>And then <code>static_cast&lt;T&gt;(thing)</code> to convert thing to type T</li>
<li>Lazy instantiations: Only member functions called are instantiated</li>
<li>Member templates cannot be virtual, can not build vtable for the class unless the entire program has been compiled</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-template-template-parameters-ttps" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#template-template-parameters-ttps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Template Template Parameters (TTPs)</h3>
<ul>
<li>Instead of providing a type, provide a template
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T, <span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> U&gt; <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">CONT</span>&gt; <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Stack</span>;</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-specialisation-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#specialisation-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Specialisation</h3>
<ul>
<li>Partial Specialisation example: provides a specialised version for pointer types
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Stack</span>&lt;T*&gt; {
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
  <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">push</span>(T*);
  <span class="pl-k">void</span> T* <span class="pl-en">pop</span>();
  T* <span class="pl-en">top</span>() <span class="pl-k">const</span>;
  <span class="pl-k">bool</span> <span class="pl-en">empty</span>() <span class="pl-k">const</span>;
<span class="pl-k">private:</span>
  std::vector&lt;T*&gt; stack_;
};</pre></div>
</li>
<li>This implementation will be used for <code>Stack&lt;int*&gt; s;</code></li>
<li>Specialising members but not the class</li>
<li>Vector of bool iterator are not dereferencable</li>
<li>at vs [] - at is exception safe</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-type-traits" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#type-traits"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Type Traits</h3>
<ul>
<li>A <strong>trait</strong> is a class or class template that characterises a type</li>
<li>Get the type:
<ul>
<li><code>using T = decltype(*begin);</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The STL <code>type_traits</code>
<ul>
<li><code>is_void</code>, <code>is_integral</code>, <code>is_class</code>, <code>is_pointer</code>, etc</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-type-transformation" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#type-transformation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Type Transformation</h4>
<ul>
<li>Fix so it works with references</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">remove_reference</span> {
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> type = T;
};

<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">remove_reference</span>&lt;T&amp;&gt; {
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> type = T;
};

<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-c1">remove_reference_t</span> = <span class="pl-k">typename</span> remove_reference&lt;T&gt;::type;

<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> U&gt;
<span class="pl-k">auto</span> <span class="pl-en">findmin</span>(U bgin, U end) {
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> T = <span class="pl-c1">remove_reference_t</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">decltype</span>(*begin)&gt;;
  <span class="pl-k">auto</span> min = std::numeric_limits&lt;T&gt;::<span class="pl-c1">min</span>();
}
</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Check type</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">is_numeric</span> {
  <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">bool</span> value = <span class="pl-c1">false</span>;
};

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Specialisation</span>
<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;&gt;
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">is_numeric</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">int</span>&gt; {
  <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">bool</span> value = <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
};</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Should not use if statement for precondition, use assert</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-en">static_assert</span>(is_numeric&lt;T&gt;::value, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Value must be numeric<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Overload <code>operator bool()</code> so can treat it as bool</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">is_numeric</span> {
  <span class="pl-k">constexpr</span> <span class="pl-k">operator</span> <span class="pl-en">bool</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> value;
  }
  <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">bool</span> value = <span class="pl-c1">false</span>;
};</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><strong>Trailing return type</strong></li>
</ul>
<pre><code>template &lt;typename It&gt;
auto fcn (It beg, It end) -&gt; decltype(*beg) {
  // loop through the range
  // return a reference to an element
  return *beg;
}
</code></pre>
<h4><a id="user-content-binding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#binding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Binding</h4>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Refernce type</th>
<th>rvalue</th>
<th>const rvalue</th>
<th>lvalue</th>
<th>const lvalue</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>T&amp;&amp;</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>const T&amp;&amp;</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>T&amp;</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td>yes</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>const T&amp;</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td>yes</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>template T&amp;&amp;</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td>yes</td>
<td>yes</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ul>
<li><code>const T&amp;</code> binds to everythin so we use it a lot</li>
<li><code>T&amp;&amp;</code> binds only to non-const rvalues</li>
</ul>
<h5><a id="user-content-reference-collapsing" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#reference-collapsing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Reference Collapsing</h5>
<ul>
<li><code>T&amp; &amp;</code> becomes <code>T&amp;</code></li>
<li><code>T&amp; &amp;&amp;</code> becomes <code>T&amp;</code></li>
<li><code>T&amp;&amp; &amp;</code> becomes <code>T&amp;</code></li>
<li><code>T&amp;&amp; &amp;&amp;</code> becomes <code>T&amp;&amp;</code></li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-forwarding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#forwarding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Forwarding</h4>
<ul>
<li><code>std::forward</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
T&amp;&amp; forward(<span class="pl-k">typename</span> remove_reference&lt;T&gt;::type&amp; a) <span class="pl-k">noexcept</span> {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">static_cast</span>&lt;T&amp;&amp;&gt;(a);
}</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>forward&lt;T&gt;(a)</code> is equivalent to
<ul>
<li><code>static_cast&lt;[const]T&amp;&amp;&gt;(a)</code> when a is an rvalue</li>
<li><code>static_cast&lt;[const]T&amp;&gt;(a)</code> when a is an lvalue</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Perfect Forwarding: lvalues stay as lvalues and rvalues stay as rvalues and constness is preserved</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-variadic-templates-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#variadic-templates-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Variadic Templates</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>typeinfo<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T&gt;
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-k">const</span> T&amp; msg) {
  std::cout &lt;&lt; msg &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
}

<span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> A, <span class="pl-k">typename</span>... B&gt;
<span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">print</span>(A head, B... tail) {
  <span class="pl-c1">print</span>(head);
  <span class="pl-c1">print</span>(tail...);
}</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Vector has like fill and range constructor</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Blob</span> {
  std::vector&lt;std::string&gt; v_;
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
  <span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span>... Args&gt;
  <span class="pl-en">Blob</span>(Args&amp;&amp;... args) : v_(std::forward&lt;Args&gt;(args)...) { }
};</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-week-8" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#week-8"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Week 8</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-iterator-traits" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#iterator-traits"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Iterator Traits</h3>
<ul>
<li>Traits define/desscribe the class properties for an iterator</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> It&gt;
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">MyIt</span> {
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> difference_type = std::<span class="pl-c1">ptrdiff_t</span>;
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> iterator_category = std::forward_iterator_tag;
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> value_type = T;
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> pointer = T*;
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> reference = T&amp;;
};</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-enable_if-and-sfinae" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#enable_if-and-sfinae"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><code>enable_if</code> and SFINAE</h3>
<ul>
<li><code>static_assert</code> will fail in compile time</li>
<li>Use <code>enable_if</code> if want to have functions to run under specific condition</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-k">template</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T1, <span class="pl-k">typename</span> T2&gt;
std::<span class="pl-c1">enable_if_t</span>&lt;std::is_same&lt;T1, T2&gt;{}, <span class="pl-k">bool</span>&gt;
<span class="pl-en">check_type</span>(<span class="pl-k">const</span> T1&amp; t1, <span class="pl-k">const</span> T2&amp; t2) {
  std::cout &lt;&lt; t1 &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> and <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t2 &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> are same type<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
}

&lt;<span class="pl-k">template</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> T1, <span class="pl-k">typename</span> T2&gt;
std::<span class="pl-c1">enable_if_t</span>&lt;!std::is_same&lt;T1, T2&gt;{}, <span class="pl-k">bool</span>&gt;
<span class="pl-en">check_type</span>(<span class="pl-k">const</span> T1&amp; t1, <span class="pl-k">const</span> T2&amp; t2) {
  std::cout &lt;&lt; t1 &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> and <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> &lt;&lt; t2 &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> are same type<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
}</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>enable_if</code> is an example of Substituion Failure Is Not An Error (SFINAE) which disable a function overload and backtracks to find another function overload that will compile</li>
<li>If no function is found than an error will be generated</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">struct</span> <span class="pl-en">EV</span> {
  <span class="pl-k">template </span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> RandomIt, <span class="pl-k">typename</span> = std::<span class="pl-c1">enable_if_t</span>&lt;std::is_arithmetic&lt;<span class="pl-k">typename</span> std::iterator_traits&lt;RandomIt&gt;::value_type&gt;{}&gt;&gt;
  <span class="pl-en">EV</span>(RandomIt begin, RandomIt end) {
    std::cout &lt;<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> hi<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
  }
};</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-week-9" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#week-9"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Week 9</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-multithreading" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#multithreading"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Multithreading</h3>
<ul>
<li>Common types of program workloads:
<ul>
<li>Sequential</li>
<li>Parallel</li>
<li>Embarassingly parallel</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Memory Models
<ul>
<li>Shared memory - all threads share the same memory</li>
<li>Local memory - each thread has it's own exclusive memory</li>
<li>Message Passing - each thread has it's own memory and can share data with other threads by sending them data objects through messages</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-race-condiditon" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#race-condiditon"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Race condiditon</h4>
<ul>
<li>Multiple threads with shared resources can have race condition</li>
<li><code>std::thread</code> takes in a function
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>std::thread t1{[&amp;] {
  <span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> j = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; j &lt; num; ++j) {
    i++;
  }
}};</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>And then do <code>t1.join();</code> wait for t1 to finish</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Mutual Exclusion: Critical Section</li>
<li>Part of code when accessing shared resources</li>
<li>Use a Mutex to allow only one thread at a time access the critical section</li>
<li>Mutex is an object shared between threads</li>
<li><strong>Deadlock</strong>
<ul>
<li>When threads can not make any progress because can not acquire resource</li>
<li>Fix by resource ordering</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-atomic-operations" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#atomic-operations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Atomic Operations</h4>
<ul>
<li>Generally takes 1 CPU cycle</li>
<li><code>std::atomic</code> does not provide support for your own data types</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-mutex" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mutex"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Mutex</h4>
<ul>
<li>in <code>&lt;mutex&gt;</code> header file</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>std::mutex blah;
blah.lock();
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> critical section</span>
blah.unlock();</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Can not copy the mutex, would not compile (copy ctor is not defined)</li>
<li>Possible bug: not unlock-ing after throwing exception</li>
<li>Solution: use lock guard
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>std::lock_guard&lt;std::mutex&gt; <span class="pl-en">guard</span>(blah);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>lock guard got destroyed when out of scope, the destructor unlocks the mutex</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Use <code>std::recursive_lock</code> for recursive code</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-unique-lock" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#unique-lock"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Unique Lock</h4>
<ul>
<li>Resource ordering when need to acquire multiple locks
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">bool</span> acquired = <span class="pl-c1">false</span>;
<span class="pl-k">while</span> (!acquired) {
  lock1.<span class="pl-c1">lock</span>();
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> (lock2.<span class="pl-c1">try_lock</span>()) {
    acquired = <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
  } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
    lock1.<span class="pl-c1">unlock</span>();
  }
}</pre></div>
</li>
<li>So use Unique lock
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>std::unique_lock&lt;std::mutex&gt; <span class="pl-en">lock1</span>(from.m, std::defer_lock);
std::unique_lock&lt;std::mutex&gt; <span class="pl-en">lock2</span>(to.m, std::defer_lock);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> lock both at the same time</span>
<span class="pl-en">std::lock</span>(lock1, lock2);</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-week-10" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#week-10"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Week 10</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-condition-variable" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#condition-variable"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Condition Variable</h3>
<ul>
<li>Producer Consumer problem
<ul>
<li>Example: bounded buffer, worker consumer, web server</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Allows threads to block, release a mutex and wait until data is set by another thread or until a time period has elapsed</li>
<li>Condition variables for producer consumer:
<ul>
<li><code>hasMaterials</code></li>
<li><code>hasCapacity</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Using the condition variable</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre>std::condition_variable hasCapacity;

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> inside the producer</span>
std::unique_lock&lt;std::mutex&gt; <span class="pl-en">lg</span>(materialsCountMutex);
hasCapacity.wait(lg, [<span class="pl-c1">this</span>, &amp;i] {
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> (materialsCount + i &gt; CAPCITY)
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span>;
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
});
materialsCount += i;
hasMaterials.notify_one();</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>std::async</code>
<ul>
<li>Function returning a <code>std::future</code></li>
<li><code>std::future</code> is a thing where you can check if the result is available yet</li>
<li><code>std::launch::async</code> - to launch a new thread</li>
<li>Good to use for exception handling too
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre> <span class="pl-k">try</span> {
   <span class="pl-k">int</span> res = future.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>();
 } <span class="pl-k">catch</span> (<span class="pl-k">const</span> std::exception&amp; ex) {
   std::cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>something<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
 }</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-object-oriented-programming-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#object-oriented-programming-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Object Oriented Programming</h3>
<h3><a id="user-content-inheritance" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#inheritance"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Inheritance</h3>
<ul>
<li>Ability to create new classes based on existing ones</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Book</span> { ... };
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Disc_book</span>: <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-en">Book</span> {... };</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>public</code> is the same as Java's <code>extends</code></li>
<li><code>private</code> cannot be accessed by user code and also derived class</li>
<li><code>protected</code> - derived classes can access</li>
<li>If <code>class Square: private Shape {...};</code> user can not access the code</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-memory-layout" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#memory-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Memory Layout</h3>
<ul>
<li>Up-casting: child to parent</li>
<li>Down-casting: parent to child</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-polymorphism" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#polymorphism"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Polymorphism</h3>
<ul>
<li>Allows objects of a class to be used as if they were object of another class</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-dynamic-binding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dynamic-binding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Dynamic binding</h3>
<ul>
<li>Run-time resolution of the appropriate function to invoke based on the type of the object</li>
<li>static type: the type the compiler sees (compile-time)</li>
<li>dynamic type: the actual type (run-time)</li>
<li>If not pointer then the static and dynamic type are always the same</li>
<li><code>virtual</code>: determine at run-time what type this is, to decide which function to call</li>
<li>Object is sliced when child object become a type of parent</li>
<li><code>static_cast</code> - undefined behaviour</li>
<li><code>dynamic_cast</code> - throw exception for different class (if reference)
<ul>
<li>If pointer, returns a <code>nullptr</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Can not just copy parent to child</li>
<li>Put <code>override</code> in child class member function that overrides the one in base class
<ul>
<li><code>double area() override { ... }</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Can also ask the compiler to provide it for you in the base class
<ul>
<li><code>virtual double area() = 0;</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Need to define destructor as virtual
<ul>
<li><code>virtual ~Shape() = default;</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Member functions
<ul>
<li><strong>Pure virtual</strong>
<ul>
<li><code>virtual void draw() = 0;</code></li>
<li>Inherit interface only</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Virtual</strong>
<ul>
<li><code>virtual void draw();</code></li>
<li>Inherit interface and optional implementation</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Non virtual</strong>
<ul>
<li><code>std::string isbn();</code></li>
<li>Inherit implementation and mandatory implementation</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>final</code> - put this instead of <code>override</code> if the subclasses should not override</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-week-11" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#week-11"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Week 11</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-polymorphism-and-dynamic-binding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#polymorphism-and-dynamic-binding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Polymorphism and Dynamic Binding</h3>
<ul>
<li>Static binding for nonvirtuals</li>
<li>Dynamic binding for virtuals</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-c-object-model" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#c-object-model"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>C++ Object Model</h3>
<ul>
<li>Not represented in object: static data members, static member functions, nonvirtual functions</li>
<li>Represented in an object: non static data members, virtual functions</li>
<li>Each polymorphic class has a virtual table, called <strong>vtable</strong> containing the address for all the virtual functions</li>
<li>Each object has a hidden virtual pointer <strong>vptr</strong>, pointing to the beginning of its vtable</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-example-vtable" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#example-vtable"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Example vtable</h4>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">A</span> {                 vtable <span class="pl-k">for</span> A: [<span class="pl-c1">0</span> | &amp;A:f(<span class="pl-k">int</span>) ]
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>                                 [<span class="pl-c1">1</span> | &amp;A:g()    ]
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">f</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span>);
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">g</span>();
};
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">B</span> : <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-en">A</span> {      vtable <span class="pl-k">for</span> B: [<span class="pl-c1">0</span> | &amp;B:f(<span class="pl-k">int</span>) ]
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>                                 [<span class="pl-c1">1</span> | &amp;A:g()    ]
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">f</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span>);                  [<span class="pl-c1">2</span> | &amp;B:h()    ]
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">h</span>();
};
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">C</span> : <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-en">B</span> {      vtable <span class="pl-k">for</span> C: [<span class="pl-c1">0</span> | &amp;B:f(<span class="pl-k">int</span>) ]
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>                                 [<span class="pl-c1">1</span> | &amp;A:g()    ]
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">x</span>();                      [<span class="pl-c1">2</span> | &amp;B:h()    ]
};                                      [<span class="pl-c1">3</span> | &amp;C:x()    ]</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-name-hiding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#name-hiding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Name Hiding</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Fruit</span> {
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">eat</span>(<span class="pl-k">float</span> f) { std::cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>F::e, <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>; }
};

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Apple</span> : <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-en">Fruit</span> {
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">eat</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> i) { std::cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>A::e, <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>; }
};</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>With the code above, the <code>eat(int)</code> override the one with float</li>
<li><strong>Overloading</strong>: same scope, same name but different signatures</li>
<li><strong>Overriding</strong>: same name, same signature but different scopes (covariant return types)</li>
<li>To fix it, <code>using</code>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Apple</span> : <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-en">Fruit</span> {
<span class="pl-k">public:</span>
  <span class="pl-k">using</span> Fruit::eat;
  <span class="pl-k">virtual</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">eat</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> i) { std::cout &lt;&lt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>A::e, <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>; }
}<span class="pl-ii"></span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-covariants-and-contravariants" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#covariants-and-contravariants"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Covariants and Contravariants</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>Covariants</strong>: what should return types of overriding function be?</li>
<li><strong>Contravariants</strong>: what should parameter types of overriding function be?</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-initialisation-and-destruction" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#initialisation-and-destruction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Initialisation and Destruction</h3>
<ul>
<li>For example if <code>class Book</code> extended by <code>class Disc_book</code> and extended again by <code>class Bulk_Disc_book</code>, then the order is
<ul>
<li>Book</li>
<li>Disc_book</li>
<li>Bulk_Disc_book</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>And with each suboject:
<ul>
<li>The data members initialised in declaration order</li>
<li>The class' constructor is called</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The reverse for destructors</li>
<li>Virtual destructor means the class does not get synthsised move operations</li>
</ul>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>
